✅❌✅—✅❌✅|✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅`✅❌✅—✅❌✅f✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅_✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅v✅❌✅—✅❌✅_✅❌✅—✅❌✅f✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅`✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅|✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅2✅❌✅—✅❌✅5✅❌✅—✅❌✅,✅❌✅—✅❌✅7✅❌✅—✅❌✅6✅❌✅—✅❌✅9✅❌✅—✅❌✅.✅❌✅—✅❌✅9✅❌✅—✅❌✅4✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅|✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅7✅❌✅—✅❌✅7✅❌✅—✅❌✅0✅❌✅—✅❌✅.✅❌✅—✅❌✅0✅❌✅—✅❌✅0✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅|✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅2✅❌✅—✅❌✅.✅❌✅—✅❌✅9✅❌✅—✅❌✅%✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅|✅❌✅—✅❌✅✅❌✅—✅❌✅
✅❌✅—✅❌✅|✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅`✅❌✅—✅❌✅f✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅_✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅m✅❌✅—✅❌✅_✅❌✅—✅❌✅b✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅y✅❌✅—✅❌✅`✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅|✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅1✅❌✅—✅❌✅,✅❌✅—✅❌✅4✅❌✅—✅❌✅2✅❌✅—✅❌✅0✅❌✅—✅❌✅.✅❌✅—✅❌✅4✅❌✅—✅❌✅7✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅|✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅3✅❌✅—✅❌✅,✅❌✅—✅❌✅5✅❌✅—✅❌✅6✅❌✅—✅❌✅1✅❌✅—✅❌✅.✅❌✅—✅❌✅5✅❌✅—✅❌✅0✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅|✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅7✅❌✅—✅❌✅1✅❌✅—✅❌✅.✅❌✅—✅❌✅5✅❌✅—✅❌✅%✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅|✅❌✅—✅❌✅✅❌✅—✅❌✅

✅❌✅—✅❌✅#✅❌✅—✅❌✅#✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅T✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅p✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅C✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅i✅❌✅—✅❌✅b✅❌✅—✅❌✅u✅❌✅—✅❌✅t✅❌✅—✅❌✅o✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅s✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅(✅❌✅—✅❌✅b✅❌✅—✅❌✅y✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅R✅❌✅—✅❌✅T✅❌✅—✅❌✅C✅❌✅—✅❌✅ ✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅a✅❌✅—✅❌✅r✅❌✅—✅❌✅n✅❌✅—✅❌✅e✅❌✅—✅❌✅d✅❌✅—✅❌✅)✅❌✅—✅❌✅✅❌✅—✅❌✅
